 Lok Sabha Elections 2019 LIVE: Rann of power, first phase, Congress won 91 seats in 20 states in 1971 also
 1977, 80, 84 main yahaan se congress candidet jagannatha raav ne apana paracham buland kiya
 Gopinath Gajapati of Congress was elected from here in 1989 and 91
 1996 main yahaan se purv PM pivi narsimha raav congress ummidavaar ke taur par jite
 Actually Narasimha Rao also won from Nandyal in Andhra in 1996, but he retained his candidature from this seat
 1998 ke loksabhaa ellection main bhi yahaan congress kaa hi dabadabaa rahaa or jayanti patnayak vijay rath par savaar hue
 In 1999, BJP opened its account on this seat
 anandi charan sahu ne yahaan camel khilaayaa
 In 2004, the Congress returned and Chandra Shekhar Sahu was the leader in the election race
 haalanki 2009 main biju janata dal ne is seat par ghuspaith kar hi lee
 Siddhant Mahapatra won this seat
 2014 main bhi unki seat kaa silsilaa barkaraar rahaa
 Jammu and Kashmir, Maharashtra Voting LIVE: Voting started on 7 seats in Maharashtra and 2 seats of JK
 The BJD, which entered this seat in 2009, has established its roots in the region by 2014
 2014 main biju janata dal ke siddhant mahapatra ko 3 lakh 98 hajaar 107 vot mili
 He won the election with 127720 votes
 duusare number par rahe congress ke chandra shekhar sahu ko 270387 vot mili
 BJP stood at number three on this seat
 party candidet ramchandra pandas ko 158811 vot mili
 However, in Odisha, BJP is pushing for victory in the Lok Sabha and Assembly elections
 bijepi kaa is rajya par kaaphi focus he
 That is why Prime Minister Narendra Modi has held several rallies in the last few months
 bijepi ko lagata he ki rajya kii satta par kai saal se kaayam bijd ke naveen patnayak ko bedakhal karne kaa acha mauka he
 Therefore, the party is showing no hesitation in taking the hands of BJD leaders
 bijepi baijayant pandas sahit bijd ke kai saasandon ko party kii sadsyta dilaa chuki he
 These include BJD MP from Bhadrak and former Union Minister Arjun Sethi, Nabrangpur MP Balabhadra Majhi, Kandhamal MP Pratyusha Rajeshwari Singh and Kalahandi MP Araka Keshari Dev
 chunaav kii har khabar milegi sidhe aapke inbox main
 To stay updated with the latest news of the general election, subscribe to Aaj Tak's election special newsletter akhil bhartiya tennis sangh (eitie) ne somvaar ko khel mantralay se mahesh bhupati or rohan bopanna ko liender pes ke saath landan olympic main khilne ko taiyaar karne ko kaha
 Newly appointed AITA Secretary General Bharat Ojha said the Sports Ministry should ask Bhupathi and Bopanna why they have refused to play with Paes
 ojha ke mutabik agar bhupati or bopanna sarkaar dwaara di ja rahi raashi par prashikshan praapt kar sakate hai to ve desh ke liye khilne se inkaar nahin kar sakate
 Ojha said, "professional distances should be abolished for the sake of the country
 pes or bhupati ke bich lambe samay se baatcheet nahin he lekin unhone desh ke liye 20 se adhik davis cap match jite hai
 " ojha kaa yah bayaan khel mantri ajay maakan ke us bayaan ke baad aayaa he, jisamen unhone landan olympic ke liye ek purush yugal team bhejne ke eitie ke faisle par sawaal khadaa kiya he
 Maken also said why AITA wants to pair Bhupathi and Paes after they have returned empty-handed from the last four Olympic Games
 ojha ne kaha ki bhupati ke liye yah pes ke saath dooriyaan khatm karke desh ke liye kuch karne kaa sabase acha vakt he
 "ojha like this comes in other sports too, but the country is the first
" ham bhupati or pes ke bich ke masale ko samaj sakate hai lekin bopanna isse dur kyon ja rahe hai? ham bopanna se is maamle main apana paksh saaf karne ko kahenge
 " isse pehle, maakan ne twit kiya ki jab do timen landan bhejne kii gunjaaish he to phir ek team hi bhejne kii taiyaari kyon kii ja rahi he
 On this controversy related to Indian tennis, Maken has tweeted, "we can send two teams, then why send one? The biggest question is who will support Sania? Why are we spoiling the Grand Slam winning pair?" ? " eitie ne shuukravaar ko kaha ki liender pes or mahesh bhupati yugal muqablon main khelenge lekin bhupati ne pes ke saath khilne se inkaar kar diya
 The Sangh then paired Rohan Bopanna with Paes but on Monday he too denied it
 bharat kii do jodiyaan olympic main khel sakati hai kyonki vishwa ke saatven variyata praapt khilaadi pes swaabhaavik taur par olympic ke liye kwalifai kar chuke hai jabaki bhupati or bopanna kii saatvin variyata praapt jodi ek team ke taur par olympic main khilne kaa adhikaar rakhti he
 AITA, however, is adamant about sending a team
 uskaa kahana he ki pes ke saath chaahe jo bhi khele lekin yah jodi olympic main desh ko padak dilaa sakati he
 It is to be decided on 21 June whether Sania Mirza will get a wildcard for the mixed doubles
 iske baad hi eitie sania or bhupati ko is varg main utaarne ko lekar koi faisla karegaa
 Prior to Maken's tweet, India's doubles specialist Bopanna refused to play with Paes, following in the footsteps of his regular partner Bhupathi
 bopanna ne ek bayaan jari kar apni raay spasht kii
 In his letter to AITA, Bopanna made it clear that he did not want to play with Paes
 haalanki bopanna ne yah bhi saaf kiya ki olympic main bharat kaa pratinidhitiv karnaa unka sapana rahaa he
 Bhupathi had said last week that he did not want to pair with Paes
 bhupati kaa yah bayaan eitie dwaara unhen pes kaa jodidar banaae jane ke kuch samay baad hi aayaa tha
 The comments bopanna ne likhaa he, "ham sangh ke faisle kaa sammaan karte hai lekin main philhal sangh kaa pes ke saath khilne sambandhi faisla maanane kii sthiti main nahin hum
 i have given information to the Sangh in this regard
 " Bopanna said that earlier this year he teamed up with Bhupathi simply because he wanted to play for the country in the Olympics
 bopanna ke mutabik vah tathaa pes acha jodi nahin banaate or isse koi parinaam nahin nikalne vaala he

 i have given information to the Sangh in this regard
 " Bopanna said that earlier this year he teamed up with Bhupathi simply because he wanted to play for the country in the Olympics
 bopanna ke mutabik vah tathaa pes acha jodi nahin banaate or isse koi parinaam nahin nikalne vaala he
 Ojha's statement comes after Sports Minister Ajay Maken's statement in which he questioned aita's decision to send a men's doubles team to the London Olympics
 maakan ne yah bhi kaha ki aakhirkaar eitie bhupati or pes ko jodidar kyon bananaa chahta he jabaki ve beete chaar olympic khelon se khaali haath laute hai
 Ojha said that for Bhupathi, this is the best time to do something for the country by ending the distance with Paes
 bakaul ojha, "is tarah kii dikkatein duusare khelon main bhi aati hai lekin desh sarvapratham hota he
 We can understand the issue between Bhupathi and Paes but why is Bopanna going away from it? We will ask Bopanna to clear his stand in this matter
 " Earlier, Maken tweeted that when there is scope to send two teams to London then why are preparations being made to send only one team
 bhartiya tennis se jude is vivaad par maakan ne twit kiya he, "ham do timen bhej sakate hai to phir ek kyon bhejein? sabase bada sawaal yah he ki sania kaa saath koun degaa? ham grand slam jeetne vaali jodi ko kyon kharaab kar rahe hai?" AITA said on Friday that Leander Paes and Mahesh Bhupathi would play doubles but Bhupathi refused to play with Paes
 iske baad sangh ne pes ke saath rohan bopanna ko joda lekin somvaar ko unhone bhi isse inkaar kar diya
 Two pairs of India can play in the Olympics as world seventh seed Paes has naturally qualified for the Olympics while the seventh seeded pair of Bhupathi and Bopanna have the right to play in the Olympics as a team
 eitie, haalanki ek team hi bhejne ko lekar adig he
 He says that no matter who plays with Paes, the pair can win the country a medal in the Olympics
 21 june ko is baat kaa faisla hona he ki sania mirza ko mishrit yugal ke liye wildcard milegaa yaa nahin
 Only then will AITA decide to field Sania and Bhupathi in this category
 maakan ke is twit se pehle bharat ke yugal visheshgy bopanna ne apane niyamit jodidar bhupati ke nakshekadam par chalate hue pes ke saath khilne se inkaar kar diya
 Bopanna issued a statement clarifying his opinion
 eitie ko likhe apane patr main bopanna ne saaf kar diya ki vah pes ke saath nahin khelnaa chaahate
 However, Bopanna also made it clear that it was his dream to represent India in the Olympics
 bhupati ne beete saptaah yah kaha tha ki vah pes ke saath jodi nahin bananaa chaahate
 Bhupathi's statement came shortly after AITA made him Pace's partner
 tippaniyan Bopanna wrote, "we respect the decision of the Sangh but i am not in a position to accept the Sangh's decision to play with Paes at the moment
" maine is sambandh main sangh ko jaankaree de di he
 " bopanna ne kaha ki is saal kii shuruyaat main unhone bhupati ke saath jodi sirf isliye banaai thi kyonki vah olympic main desh ke liye khelnaa chaahate the
 According to Bopanna, he and Paes do not make a good pair and it is not going to produce any results

 iske baad sangh ne pes ke saath rohan bopanna ko joda lekin somvaar ko unhone bhi isse inkaar kar diya

 eitie, haalanki ek team hi bhejne ko lekar adig he

 One of the ten Mahavidya forms of the Goddess is that of Mother Baglamukhi
 inhen pitaambara or brahmastra bhi kaha jaataa he
 They themselves have yellow aura and yellow color is used in their worship
 inako stambhan shakti kii devi mana jaataa he
 Lord Vishnu did penance to calm the Mahatufan that appeared in Saurashtra, and as a result of this penance, Mother Baglamukhi appeared
 shatru or virodhiyon ko shant karne ke liye tathaa mukademe main vijay ke liye inaki upasna achook he
 This time the birth anniversary of Maa Baglamukhi will be celebrated on 19 April
 maan bagalaamukhi ke puja ke niyam or saavdhaaniyaan kya hai?- inaki puja tantra kii puja he atah bina kisi guru ke nirdesan ke nahi kerani chahie- inaki puja kabhi bhi kisi ke naash ke liye na karen- inaki puja main vyakti ko pile asana, pile vastra, pile fal or pile naivaidhya kaa prayog karnaa chahie- inke mantra jaap ke liye haldi kii maala kaa prayog karen- puja kaa upyukt samay he sandhyaakaal yaa madhyaraatri- shatru or virodhiyon ko shant karne ke liye, bagalaamukhi janmotsav par inaki puja jarur karen

 yah salanaa college entrens ejamination he jo iity main daakhile ke liye hota he
 It is said to be among the most difficult engineering entrance exams in the world
 lagbhag dedh lakh students jeii (main) paas karke jeii (advance) ke liye qualiphi hai

 silebus is samay tak khatm ho chukaa hoga
 Success Tips Before the Exam: Tips for JEE (advanced) Mathematics: 1) According to earlier g papers, more attention was needed on topics like Vector and 3D than on Probability or Indefinite Integration
 ek or chapter complex number he
 Every year 2-3 questions are asked from this chapter
 isliye complex number, vector, thri di or definit intigral main maharath hasil karnaa pehali praathamikta honi chahie
 2) If you have the ability to represent functions in graph form then algebra can be easy for you
 3)diferenshial calculas kaa equation se gaharaa sambandh he
 Especially if you use Rolls and Lagrange theorems
 4)koordinate geometry main sawaalon ko hal karne ke liye complex numbers kaa istemaal kiya ja saktaa he
 Trigonometric questions require the application of De Mowre Theorem
 5)algebra main paramuteshan—combination or probability duusare bahut mahatvapurn topic hai
 You should specialize in Bayes theorem, different methods of derangement and distribution
 inaki jarurat vahaan hoti he
 6) Integral calculus can be simplified keeping in mind the use of certain tricks and some basic variations of integral functions
 property ko yaad rakhane or unke samajhdaari bhare istemaal se samay kii kaaphi bachat hoti he
 7) Practical knowledge and understanding of parametric form of organic geometry is very important to understand geometry
 8)antat: mathematics main acha pradarshan karne kaa ekmaatr tarika yah he ki pichley saalon main jeii ke paper main puche gaye sawaalon ko dhyaan main rakhte hue samasyaon ko sulajhaya jaae
 Tips for JEE (advanced) Chemistry: 1) Concept should be very clear
 aplicoshan skills or die gaye silebus ke bare main jaankaree par focus hona chahie
 2) To increase your speed, solve the most important numericals daily
 kuch buniyadi topic jaise mol concept, chemical equilibrium or electro chemistry par vishesh dhyaan den
 3) It is important to be very careful and restrained about organic chemistry
 sterio chemistry, jiosi (general organic chemistry) or functional group analysis par khaas dhyaan den
 4) Most of the questions asked in organic chemistry are perceptual
 in sawaalon kaa sambandh sanrachana, prakriya or prayog se hota he
 Pay special attention to chemical bonding and co-ordination chemistry
 jeii (advanced) physics ke liye tips:1)physics main makenix aisa topic he, jise zyaadaatar visheshgy scoreksharag yaa number dilaane vaala nahin maanate hai
 But one aspect related to this is that this is the topic in terms of marks in which the most questions are asked in the JEE paper
 isliye is topic ko nazarandaaj nahin kiya ja saktaa
 2) But to ensure better performance, attention should also be given to topics which give second marks such as optics, electricity and magnetism etc
 3)kinametics or partical dianemics makenix ke bahut mahatvapurn topic hai
 The questions related to this are always asked in JEE paper
 4)jeii ke puraane peparon main jitne sawaal puche gaye the, unke lihaaj se dekhen to makenix, electricity or magnetismo sabase ahm topic lagate hai
 5) Measurement and errors Thermodynamics Thermodynamics is very important both in terms of physics and chemistry
 isliye us par vishesh taur par dhyaan den
 6) Under optics, it would be wise to first study wave optics
 isaki vajah yah he ki re optics ke mukaable yah hissaa chota he
 So it can be read quickly
 jeii (advanced) crack karne ke saamaanya tips:1)taiyaari or exam ke samay ekaagratha banaae rakhen or sakaaratmak dhang se sochen
 2) Increase your speed
 kisi pratishthit mock test siries kii madad len, taaki aap main exam main safalataa hasil karne kaa jajba paidaa ho
 Solve previous year's IIT-JEE papers
 jis topic main kamjor hai, us par khaas dhyaan den or apane concept ko viksit karen
 3) It is very important to practice with JEE level questions
 isse aapaki taarkik or vishleshnatmak kshamta main ijapha hota he
 4) Remember that not only the quantity of time spent, but the quality also matters a lot
 isliye prayek 1-2 ghante kii padhai ke baad 5 se 10 minute kaa brake len
 Relax during the break
 apane bheetar shanti, sthirataa, aatmavishvaas or ekaagratha kii takat ko badhaane ke liye yoga karen
 5) Do not put too much burden on yourself
 har din 5 se 6 ghante kii neend bahut jaruri he
 Especially for the IIT-JEE exam, keep yourself physically and mentally healthy 3-4 days in advance
 kaam ke bich main halki-si jhpaki le lene se taazgi bani rahati he
 Also, avoid sleeping too late during the day
 6)ant main, agar aapako paper bahut mushkil lagata he to pareshaan yaa chintit na hon kyonki hameshaa saapekshik pradarshan hi myne rakhata he
 Use your best analytical power at work and be confident in your preparation

 vahiin mukhyamantri fadanvis ne kaha ki sarkaar ne hadtaal karne vaale doctoron ke pratinidhiyon se baat kii or unki sabhi maangon ko sweekaar kar liya
 Following this order of the High Court and assurances from the government, the Maharashtra Association of Resident Doctors (MARD) has asked all the doctors of the state to return to work
 hadtaal se charmarai swasthya vyavastahicourt ne apane aadesh main kaha ki ab marij ke saath 2 rishtedaar hi aspataal main entry le sakenge
 The High Court has directed the resident doctor to settle all his issues amicably with the Maharashtra government
 bataa den ki rajya ke kareeb 4,000 resident doctoron kii hadtaal kii vajah se aspataal kii vyavastha charmara gai he or vahaan marijon kii qatari lagi he
 Meanwhile, Medical Education Minister Girish Mahajan warned the demonstrating resident doctors that if the doctors did not start work by 8 pm on Wednesday night, they would lose six months of salary and face suspension
 mahila doctor par marij ke rishtedaaron kaa hamalaavahin buudhvaar raat yahaan sayan aspataal kii ek mahila doctor kii ek marij ke rishtedaaron ne kathith taur par pitayee kar di, jisase pradarshnkaree doctor or akramak ho gaye
 In the wake of incidents of attacks by relatives of patients in government hospitals, doctors demand that their security be enhanced
 doctoron ne kii suraksha kii mangapradarshnkaree doctoron ke ek pratinidhi ne kaha ki resident doctoron ko aspataal parisar ke samvedansheel sthanon par sashastr surakshakarmiyon kii jarurat he or ek alarm pranali bhi hona chahie taaki doctor surakshakarmi ko bula saken
 He said that the pass system normally run in private hospital should be strictly implemented so that the number of relatives visiting the patient can be tightened
 unhone doctoron par hamale ke maamle ko gaiyr jamaanti aparaadh banane or maamalon kii twaarit adaalaton main sunwaayee kiye jane kii jarurat bataai
 These are our demands and we are not asking for the moon
 phir bhi rajya sarkaar ise praathamikta ke aadhaar par nahin le rahi he
 The IMA had landed in support of the striking doctors, while the Indian Medical Association (IMA) also gave its support to the performance of resident doctors

 i appeal to the doctors and their organizations to end the strike and return to work
